beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActJumpPre'
  ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
    checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActJump'
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'CmnActJumpLanding'
      ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
        ifNot: Mem(IsNeutral)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal6), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifNot: Mem(Boss)
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal3)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(ExGauge1)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
        if: Mem(ObjReg1)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
      endElse: 
      if: Mem(PlayerVal1)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        if: Mem(ObjReg1)
          ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
            storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(14999)
            storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Val(14999)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal5)
          ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal1)
            ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
              ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
                checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Bloodsucking_UniverseExe'
                ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
                  isObjectActive: (STACK0)
                  if: Mem(Tmp)
                    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(-130)
                    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(-130)
                  endIf: 
                  else: 
                    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(-2)
                    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(-2)
                  endElse: 
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endElse: 
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(4999)
        storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(9999)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(1)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(2)
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      if: Mem(ExGauge0)
        checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'berserk'
        ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(-70)
            modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge1), Val(-70)
            ifNot: Mem(398)
              modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(1)
              ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(HitPoint), Val(168)
                ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(1)
                  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(0)
                  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                    modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                  endIf: 
                  else: 
                    if: Mem(HitPoint)
                      storeValue: Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                    endIf: 
                  endElse: 
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
              else: 
                ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(HitPoint), Val(84)
                  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(1)
                    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(0)
                    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                      modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                    endIf: 
                    else: 
                      if: Mem(HitPoint)
                        storeValue: Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                      endIf: 
                    endElse: 
                  endIf: 
                endIf: 
                else: 
                  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(2)
                    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(0)
                    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                      modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                    endIf: 
                    else: 
                      if: Mem(HitPoint)
                        storeValue: Mem(HitPoint), Val(1)
                      endIf: 
                    endElse: 
                  endIf: 
                endElse: 
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
    getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_NAG', 2, 157
    if: Mem(TrainingValue)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(1)
        if: Mem(IsRecoverableTypeA)
          storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Val(0)
          deactivateObjectByName: s32'BloodCharge_Obj'
          deactivateObjectByName: s32'BloodEaterObj'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(2)
        if: Mem(IsEnableNormalAttack)
          storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
          storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Val(15000)
          storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(1)
          callSubroutine: s32'Berserk_MeshSetCheck'
          deactivateObjectByName: s32'BloodCharge_Obj'
          deactivateObjectByName: s32'BloodEaterObj'
          deactivateObjectByName: s32'BloodEater_BUObj'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal3)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
        storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(0)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(1)
        storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(-10)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(2)
        storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(-20)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(CharacterAddDefenceRate), Val(-20)
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'Berserk_MeshSetCheck'
  ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal3)
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal3), Mem(PlayerVal0)

      setDefaultMeshSet: s32'Low'
      meshSetClearNameExchange: 
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'Low', s32'Low'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'High', s32'High'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'nohead', s32'nohead'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'headonly', s32'headonly'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'MS_1', s32'MS_1'
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal3), Mem(PlayerVal0)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal0), Mem(PlayerVal3)
      setDefaultMeshSet: s32'Low_Berserk'
      meshSetClearNameExchange: 
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'Low', s32'Low_Berserk'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'High', s32'High_Berserk'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'nohead', s32'nohead_Berserk'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'headonly', s32'headonly_Berserk'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei', s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_KakuseiBerser'
      meshSetNameExchange: s32'MS_1', s32'MS_1_Berserk'
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'AtkKezuriRate_High'
  ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal3)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
      chipDamagePercent: 10
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(1)
      chipDamagePercent: 15
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(2)
      chipDamagePercent: 20
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    chipDamagePercent: 35
  endElse: 
endSubroutine:
